Why Bookme?

You no longer have to stand in lines and can purchase your tickets from the comfort of your phone using a variety of digital payment methods. Get your ticket confirmations instantly via SMS and Email.

Published 21 Feb 2025
The Underrated Historic Towns and Villages You Need to Visit in Pakistan
Book Now
Pakistan has many old towns and villages with a long history. Some places are well known, but many are not. These hidden spots have old buildings, traditions, and stories from the past.
People in these villages still follow their old customs. They live in houses made of stone and clay. Their streets are small, and life moves slowly. Walking through these places feels like stepping back in time.
Many of these villages have forts, mosques, temples, and other ancient sites. Some were built hundreds of years ago. They show how people lived and worked in the past.
This blog will share some of these underrated towns and villages. Each place has something special. If you love history or want to see something different, these places are worth a visit.
1. Ganish Village, Hunza Valley


Ganish Village is the oldest settlement in Hunza and was once a key stop on the ancient Silk Road. Travelers passed through here while trading goods between Asia and Europe.
The village has centuries-old wooden mosques, watchtowers, and traditional houses. Some mosques in Ganish are over 400 years old and have been recognized for their cultural importance.
If you want to explore Hunza’s history and scenic landscapes, consider booking a Hunza private tour. You can also book a bus or flight to Gilgit, the nearest city, and stay in one of the hotels in Hunza for a comfortable trip.
2. Rohtas Fort, Punjab


Rohtas Fort is one of the strongest forts in South Asia. Sher Shah Suri built it in the 16th century. The fort was designed to protect the empire from attacks. Today, it stands as a reminder of that time.
The walls of the fort are massive. Some of them are over 30 feet high. There are many gates, tunnels, and towers inside. The stonework is detailed, and the structure is still strong. People can walk along the walls and look at the beautiful landscape around the fort.
This place is great for history lovers. Many visitors explore the fort, take pictures, and learn about its past. It is also a good spot for school trips and family visits.
3. Saidpur Village, Islamabad


Saidpur is a small village near Islamabad. It is more than 400 years old. The village has been influenced by different cultures over time. There are remains of Hindu temples and Sikh gurdwaras.
The streets of Saidpur have colorful houses and small shops. People sell traditional crafts and food here. Many tourists visit to enjoy the local culture. There are also small restaurants where visitors can eat traditional food.
Saidpur is a great place for a short trip. It is close to the city, but it feels different from modern Islamabad. The village gives a glimpse of old traditions and simple village life.
4. Gulmit Village, Gilgit-Baltistan


Gulmit is a beautiful village in the Hunza Valley. It was once the summer capital of the Hunza kingdom. The village has a rich history and breathtaking views.
There are many historical sites in Gulmit. Visitors can see old stone houses, wooden mosques, and a historic polo ground. The village also has a museum that displays old tools, clothes, and artwork from the past.
People in Gulmit speak the Wakhi language. They are known for their kindness and hospitality. Tourists enjoy walking through the village, meeting the locals, and taking in the peaceful surroundings.
5. Ranigat, Khyber Pakhtunkhwa


Ranigat is an ancient Buddhist site. It is located in the hills of Buner district. The site has stone carvings and remains of old buildings. These ruins are from the Gandhara civilization, which existed over 2,000 years ago.
Ranigat has large stupas, monasteries, and rock-cut caves. These were used for worship and meditation. The site gives a look into the Buddhist history of the region. It is an important place for archaeologists and history lovers.
Visitors need to hike to reach Ranigat. The view from the top is amazing. It is a peaceful place with a deep historical connection.
6. Kalash Valleys (Rumbur, Bumburet, and Birir), Khyber Pakhtunkhwa


The Kalash Valleys are home to the Kalash people. They have a unique culture that is different from the rest of Pakistan. The Kalash have their own language, customs, and festivals.
The valleys have wooden houses built on the hills. The people wear colorful clothes and jewelry. They celebrate festivals with dance and music. The most famous festivals are Chilam Joshi, Uchau, and Chaumos.
Tourists visit the Kalash Valleys to see their traditions. The people are welcoming and share their way of life. The valleys are also known for their natural beauty, with green mountains and flowing rivers.
7. Uch Sharif, Punjab


Uch Sharif is an ancient town with deep Islamic history. It was an important center for scholars and saints. The town has many old tombs and shrines.
The most famous tombs belong to Sufi saints. They have beautiful blue and white tiles. The designs on the tombs are detailed and artistic. Many visitors come here to see these historic buildings.
The town is quiet and peaceful. It is a good place for people who enjoy history and culture. The local markets sell handicrafts and traditional sweets.
8. Katas Raj Temples, Punjab


Katas Raj is a group of Hindu temples. They are located in the Salt Range mountains. These temples are very old and have religious importance. Many Hindu pilgrims visit this place every year.
The temples are built around a small pond. According to legend, the pond was created from the tears of Lord Shiva. The water in the pond is clear and reflects the temples.
Visitors can walk through the complex and see the ancient architecture. The carvings on the temples tell stories from Hindu mythology. This site is a great place to learn about history and religion.
9. Bhit Khori, Sindh


Bhit Khori is a small coastal village near Karachi. It is known for its beautiful beach and peaceful surroundings. Unlike other crowded beaches, this place is quiet and clean.
The people of Bhit Khori are mostly fishermen. They live in simple homes and depend on the sea for their livelihood. Visitors can see fishing boats and nets along the shore.
The beach is perfect for camping and swimming. Tourists often visit to relax and enjoy fresh seafood. The sunset at Bhit Khori is breathtaking.
10. Moola Chotok, Balochistan


Moola Chotok is a hidden valley in Balochistan. It has beautiful waterfalls and rocky hills. The place is surrounded by high mountains, making it feel like a secret paradise.
The waterfalls of Moola Chotok are the main attraction. The water is cool and fresh. Many people visit for hiking, swimming, and picnicking. The natural beauty of this place is untouched.
Reaching Moola Chotok is not easy. The journey is long, and the roads are rough. But for those who love adventure, the trip is worth it. The scenery and fresh air make it a great escape from city life.
Conclusion
Pakistan is full of historic towns and villages that many travelers overlook. These places hold stories from the past, with old buildings, cultural traditions, and stunning landscapes. From the ancient streets of Ganish Village to the spiritual sites of Uch Sharif and the peaceful beaches of Bhit Khori, each location offers something special.
If you love exploring history, now is the perfect time to plan your journey. Whether you want to visit centuries-old forts, hidden valleys, or historic temples, Bookme makes traveling easy. With tour packages available for different destinations, you can experience these places without any trouble.
Start your adventure today! Visit Bookme to book bus, train, or airline tickets, find hotels, and explore travel options—all in one place.

Why Bookme?
We are Pakistan's no.1 E-ticketing platform. We let you pre-book the best deals on your tickets for Movies, Bus Travel, Flights, Train Journeys, and Events. You no longer have to stand in lines and can purchase your tickets from the comfort of your phone using a variety of digital payment methods. Get your ticket confirmations instantly via SMS and Email.

PIA - Pakistan International Airlines
Pakistan International Airlines – PIA is the largest airline of Pakistan. The national airline of the country was previously known as “Orient Airways.” PIA has a fleet of over 35 aircraft including Boeing-777 and Airbus A-320, providing top-notch services to people all around the globe. PIA is the only international airline of Pakistan and has an extensive network of 3 different hubs located in Karachi, Lahore and Islamabad.

What does PIA stand for?
PIA is Pakistan's first international airline and it stands for “Pakistan International Airline”.

Extra Baggage Allowed
PIA offers great service to pre-book your baggage and pay for it without having to visit the counter before boarding for extra baggage allowance. You can take up to 7 kg hand baggage for your flight.
Headphones
PIA provides extra comfort to its passengers by giving them free headphones during the flight. Passengers can listen to music or watch shows to entertain themselves.
Meal is served
You can order a meal during the flight and pay for it. For long-distance journeys, PIA provides world-class delicious cuisines.
More Leg room
PIA does have spacious economy class seats, but if you want extra comfort and legroom, you can opt for business class.
Toilet in Airline
PIA always strives for a comfortable and pleasant journey. They have hygienic and clean washrooms on board which passengers can use.
PIA Flight Ticket Prices
PIA provides a safe and comfortable flight across the globe at affordable fares. PIA maintained its image by providing economical ticket prices for domestic and international flights. Other than that we have gathered a collective data of all the PIA flight ticket prices of different routes, take a look and get an idea about PIA flight ticket prices.

PIA Domestic Flights
PIA has set its standards on its home ground, Pakistan by providing domestic flights to almost 18 cities. PIA domestic flights are in great demand all over the country because of the top-notch services they provide. They offer accessibility and comfort to their passengers with economical ticket prices that's why PIA domestic flights have one of the busiest routes taken by passengers. PIA claims to be your trusted partner wherever you want to go, and they make sure to fulfill their promise. Including the busiest routes, PIA provides flight services to small districts as well. Check out the destinations of PIA domestic flights and get an idea.

PIA International Flights
After setting its roots domestically, PIA also conquered the international ground by providing its flight service to over 28 countries worldwide. PIA international flights have been the number one choice for the people of Pakistan flying internationally. Some of the international routes are listed below, so check them out and decide your next vacation spot!

PIA FAMOUS INTERNATIONAL ROUTES
Karachi to Istanbul
Islamabad to Dubai
Lahore to New York
Karachi to Jeddah
Karachi to Chicago
Islamabad to Sydney
Lahore to Doha
Lahore to Maldives
PIA Online Booking
PIA provides special family discounts, children discount, children less than 2 years free and low flight fares.The first Asian airline to introduce an auto-ticketing facility.Hence, you can easily book your PIA tickets online through Bookme website and application. We offer exceptional discounts on PIA online bookings.

Sarene Online Booking
Serene Air is the premier domestic airline of Pakistan, which was established in 2017. Its mission is to provide an exceptional flying experience to its passengers. The airline has become popular in a short time period because of its top-notch services and great aircraft.

Extra Baggage Allowed
Serene Air has set rules for baggage allowance. You can carry 40 kg (2 pieces) of baggage in the checked-in baggage allowance. The hand carry should be only 7 kg.
Headphones
Serene Air offers entertainment-filled flight journeys. You can get headphones for more personalized entertainment.
Meal is served
One of the unique aspects that differentiate Serene Air from other airlines is its menu. They have a diverse menu that changes every week, so you can enjoy a variety of meals if you are traveling frequently.
Mobile Charging
You can easily charge your electronic devices through personalized charging sockets present on every seat.
More Leg room
If you want to travel more comfortably, you can get access to Serene Plus, where you will get a spacious seat and more legroom.
Toilet in Airline
Passengers have access to clean and hygienic washrooms on board.
Serene Flight Ticket Prices
Serene Air not only has top-notch services, but they also offer pretty affordable and economical ticket prices to its passengers, making their travel plans more relaxing. Serene flight ticket prices can vary depending on the destination of your journey, as Serene Air operates both domestically and internationally. To make sure you get the best deal, you can take a look at the Serene flight ticket price data given in the table below. For more information, you can also visit Bookme.

(NOTE: prices can vary so make sure you visit Bookme before booking your ticket.)

Serene Air Domestic Flights
The airline is known for making journeys efficient and super safe with its fleets, such as the Boeing 737 and Boeing 800. It flies to six cities in Pakistan, including Islamabad, Karachi, Lahore, Peshawar, Faisalabad, and Quetta. Serene Air operates on one of the busiest domestic routes in Pakistan, and that's why the demand for Serene Air flights is quite high. You can find all domestic routes with prices and their schedules on Bookme.

Serene Air Online Booking
Book your Serene Air flight tickets online from Bookme to enjoy cheaper airfares. Follow the handy process mentioned below to book your Serene Air tickets online.
1. Open the Bookme app or website and go to the flight's page.
2. Select your destination, departure, and date of travel and search the query.
3. Select your flight from the available Serene Air flights.
4. Enter your personal details, i.e., name, number, ID card number, and mail address.
5. Checkout and pay through JazzCash, EasyPasa, debit/credit card, or bank transfer.

Air Blue
AirBlue is Pakistan’s 2nd largest airline, operating on both domestic and international routes. AirBlue was launched in 2003 and commenced its commercial operations on 18th June 2004. AirBlue’s fleet consists of next-generation Airbus A320 and A321 Neo Aircraft. Besides its highly affordable fares, it offers quality services and great hospitality for its passengers. AirBlue has one of the highest numbers of domestic flights and has always been the first choice of customers.

Extra Baggage Allowed
AirBlue has set different policies on extra baggage allowances for both domestic and international flights.
Headphones
AirBlue provides headphones to its passengers on board.
Ordering a meal
AirBlue does not serve meals on domestic flights however you can pre order a meal of your choice and pay for it.
Mobile Charging
AirBlue has personalized mobile charging sockets on every seat, so you can easily charge your devices.
Recliner seat
To make your journey more comfortable, AirBlue has comfortable recliner seats, which can also give you extra legroom if needed.
Toilet in Airline
Hygienic and clean washrooms are present on AirBlue airlines.

Emirates - Dubai’s Luxurious Airline
Dubai’s leading airline, Emirates Airlines, started its operations in 1985 with just two aircraft, and today, it has the largest fleet of Airbus A380s and Boeing 777s in the world. It is also the largest airline in the Middle East. This Dubai-based airline flies to more than 155 destinations in 80 countries. Over 1500 Emirates flights leave from Dubai to six continents every week. With an articulate cabin crew and Arab-inspired cuisine, expect world-class travel with Emirates

Etihad Airways - The Airline of Choices
Etihad Airways is the second-largest airline in the Middle East. Established in 2003, the UAE’s premier airline has its headquarters in Khalifa City in Abu Dhabi. The airline has an impressive portfolio of commercial, cargo, and special Etihad holidays.

Qatar Airways Online Booking, 10% off Qatar Airways Tickets
Established in 1993, Qatar Airways is well-known for its “unrivaled level of service.” The airline is the state-owned flag carrier of Qatar that operates flights from its hub, Hamad International Airport, at Doha. With its latest fleet, gourmet meals, and comfortable seating, you will have an overall fantastic experience.

AirSial
AirSial is the story of Sialkot International Airport Ltd's remarkable success. It was launched by the Sialkot Chamber of Commerce and Industry in August 2015. Currently, they have a fleet of three A320 planes with a capacity of 180 passengers each.

Extra Baggage Allowed
AirSial has one of the most generous baggage allowance policies. Passengers can carry as many bags as they want, but the total weight of bags should be up to 32 kg. Carry-on baggage should be 7 kg, and checked-in baggage should be 20 kg.
Headphones
AirSial provides headphones to all the passengers on board.
Meal is Served
AirSial has an extensive meal plan. They serve fresh and delicious meals onboard.
Mobile Charging
Separate charging ports are available on all the seats so that passengers can charge their devices easily.
AirSial Flight Ticket Prices
AirSial has been one of those consistent airlines that have kept their flight ticket prices within the economic range. Be it international or domestic flights, AirSial flight ticket prices are mostly pocket-friendly compared to other airlines. Although ticket prices can vary greatly depending on your destination, timing of the flight, or whether you're taking a direct flight or have layovers, we have gathered AirSial flight ticket prices in a table mentioned below.

(NOTE: ticket prices vary so make sure to check live prices on Bookme before booking.)
Departure Arrival Ticket Price
Islamabad (ISB) Karachi (KHI) 28866/- PKR
Lahore (LHE) Karachi (KHI) 14992/- PKR
Karachi (KHI) Islamabad (ISB) 17289/- PKR
Karachi (KHI) Jeddah (JED) 80588/- PKR
Islamabad (ISB) Muscat (MCT) 64581/- PKR
AirSial Domestic Flights
AirSial is currently operational in Pakistan and offers domestic flights. It covers major domestic routes, which include the main cities, i.e., Lahore, Karachi, and Islamabad. AirSial has become the number one choice for passengers when flying domestically because not only does AirSial provide a safe and secure environment for traveling, but they also have great on-board staff that will help you throughout your journey in case you need anything.

AirSial Online Booking
AirSial provides an exceptional airline traveling experience at economical rates with exclusive deals on online bookings. You can book your AirSial tickets online through the Bookme website and mobile application to get discounts on your tickets.
How do I book your AirSial ticket online through Bookme?
Go to the Bookme website or open the Bookme app.
Select your departure date and your destination. Also, select your departure city/airport.
Choose from the available AirSial flights.
Enter your personal details, name, number, and email address.
Pay for your booking through online payment methods like JazzCash, EasyPaisa, debit/credit card, and bank transfer. Your booking is done.
Extra Baggage Allowed

Headphones

Meal is Served
AirSial has an extensive meal plan. They serve fresh and delicious meals onboard.
Mobile Charging
Separate charging ports are available on all the seats so that passengers can charge their devices easily.

Fly Jinnah
Fly Jinnah is going to be the fourth private airline in Pakistan, launched in June 2022. The airline is a joint venture of Lakson Group and Air Arabia. Lakson Group is Pakistan's largest business conglomerate, which operates in multiple industries.

How can I make an online booking for a Fly Jinnah flight?
You can easily do online booking of Fly Jinnah flights by simply visiting the Bookme website or downloading the Bookme app.
You can easily do online booking of Fly Jinnah flights by simply visiting the Bookme website or downloading the Bookme app.
What is the luggage allowance policy for Fly Jinnah flights?
Does Fly Jinnah serve meals on flights?
Fly Jinnah operate on international flights?
How do I check my flight details after booking my seat online?

Earn Points to level up
Collect points on every booking, level up, and redeem exciting rewards!
Login
Earn Points to level up
Collect points on every booking, level up, and redeem exciting rewards!
Deals
FlyJinnah offers one of the best flying deals to its customers. They have multiple category fares that cater to the needs of almost all types of passengers. They have a variety of deals and discounts, which you can avail of by visiting their website.
Extra Baggage Allowed
The baggage allowance policy depends on the fare type you opt for. Standard fare gives you the allowance of 7 kg hand-carry baggage and 20 kg check-in baggage. If you go for premium options, you can carry more luggage.
Wifi
Fly Jinnah has an in-flight streaming service known as “Sky Time,” which allows you to connect to the local server in flight on your devices, where you can watch movies, and documentaries, and listen to your favorite music.
Headphones
Fly Jinnah provides headphones to its passengers.
Meal is Served
For meal services, Fly Jinnah offers to pre-order your meal before the flight. You can also order meals according to your choice on board and pay right there. Other than that, Fly Jinnah has a variety of world-famous, delicious meal options that you can avail of through their website.
Mobile Charging
Separate charging ports are available on every seat, so passengers can easily get access and charge their devices.
More Legroom
Fly Jinnah has comfortable and spacious seats so passengers can travel comfortably.
Add Seats
You can pre-select the seat of your choice prior to your flight. Reserve your preferred seat with Fly Jinnah and travel without any inconvenience.
Toilet in Airline
YFly Jinnah has a clean and hygienic toilet facility on board.
Fly Jinnah Airline Ticket Price
Fly Jinnah is the first airline in Pakistan with the cheapest domestic flights, as claimed by Lakson Group and Air Arabia. Fly Jinnah offers 4 different types of fare categories, and you can easily avail of them on the Fly Jinnah website. Fly Jinnah airline ticket price categories include:
Basic Fare
Value Fare
Value Flex Fare
Ultimate Fare option
All these options have different luggage policies and meal plans. From economy to luxury travel services, Fly Jinnah gives customers the power to choose packages according to their preferences and budget. We have gathered some of the most common domestic and international routes Fly Jinnah ticket prices in the table mentioned below. Take a look.

(NOTE: these prices are concluded from the data currently available.)
Departure Arrival Ticket Price
Lahore (LHE) Karachi (KHI) 17250/- PKR
Karachi (KHI) Islamabad (ISB) 23846/- PKR
Karachi (KHI) Doha (DOH) 61895/- PKR
Lahore (LHE) Muscat (MCT) 78615/- PKR
Karachi (KHI) Quetta (UET) 23390/- PKR
Islamabad (ISB) Quetta (UET) 18784/- PKR
Fly Jinnah Domestic Flights
Fly Jinnah is currently operating in 8 cities in Pakistan. Fly Jinnah has been the pioneer airline on domestic flights and has become the number one choice of customers. Fly Jinnah domestic flights have multiple cities on its radar, and these cities are Lahore (LHE), Karachi (KHI), Islamabad (ISB), Multan (MUX), Peshawar (PEW), Quetta (UET), Sialkot (SKT), and Faisalabad (LYP).

Fly Jinnah International Flights
After getting launched, Fly Jinnah was only operating domestically, but now it has opened its doors for international flights as well. In collaboration with AirArabia, Fly Jinnah international flights have gained popularity. Fly Jinnah operates in more than 15 countries through AirArabia. Fly Jinnah International Flight has been operating in Oman, Malaysia, and Sharjah.

Jazeera Airways Online Booking
Al Jazeera Airways, a Kuwaiti airline founded in 2004, was the Middle East's first privately owned airline. Since then, it has evolved to become the largest airline operating out of Kuwait, servicing destinations around the Middle East. The airline is a publicly listed corporation and an IATA member.

Malindo Air Booking
Malindo Air is a premium airline based in Malaysia, with its main office in Petaling Jaya, Selangor. The name Malindo, which is a combination of the names Malaysia and Indonesia, denotes an agreement of cooperation between the two nations. Malindo Air is based in Subang, Selangor, Malaysia, and serves both Kuala Lumpur International Airport (KLIA) and Sultan Abdul Aziz Shah Airport (commonly known as the Subang Airport, Subang SkyPark, or LTSAAS).

Oman Air Booking
Oman Air Booking is now available on Bookme. Want to know more about them? It is known for providing quality, ultramodern service on its flights, as well as outstanding interiors in its aircraft. Its fleet consists of about 30 flights, including Airbus A330-300, Boeing 787-9, and Boeing 737-800 aircraft. By serving various destinations throughout the world, the airline has helped to make Muscat a transport center for tourism, business, and more in the Middle East.

Srilankan Airlines Booking
Srilankan Airlines provides up to 100 flights per week to 11 destinations. After severing ties with Emirates and as a result of the frequent flyer program, Srilankan Airlines introduced FlySmiles, its own frequent flyer program, in 2008.

Saudi Airline
The Saudi Airline previously famous as “Saudi Arabian Airline” has embarked its success in the Airline industry through great customer service and providing luxurious travel experience to passengers. Started with a single twin-engine DC-3 back in 1945 that was gifted to King Abdul Aziz by U.S president Franklin D.roosevelt, it has become a world famous Airline operating company.

Thai Airways
Thai Airways (Thailand Airlines) is a public airline registered in 1991 under Securities Exchange of Thailand, with the Ministry of France holding the shares up to 50%. Thai Airways was created to cater the public needs for domestic as well as international flights.

Air Arabia
Air Arabia also known as Air Al Arabia is the first low-cost airline, launched in October 2003 and located in the Middle East has gained significant popularity in the past few years. The airline headquarter is located at Sharjah freight center, and Sharjah International Airport is the main hub for Air Arabia flying operations.

Gulf Air Airlines
Gulf Air was launched in 1950 and has been the flag bearer for Bahrain for several years. Being the first international airline launched by the Bahrain government, Golf Air has become the epitome of success in a few years. Gulf Air has its headquarters in Muharraq and operates from Bahrain International Airport.

China Southern Airlines
China Southern Airlines is a subsidiary of China Southern Air Holding Company Ltd and has been providing air transportation services for several years. China Southern Airlines carries out its operations from its headquarters located in Guangzhou, Guangdong Province. This airline is also known as “CSN,” a short form for China Southern Airlines. China Southern Airlines has set its standards by prioritizing customers’ needs first. China Southern Airlines has been providing its services by having a top-notch fleet of aircraft, which includes Boeing’s 787, 777, and 737 series, Airbus’ a350, 330, and 320 series, and COMAC’s ARJ-21 and C919.

Azal Air - Azerbaijan Airlines
Azal Azerbaijan Airlines, also known as Azal Airlines, is the first international airline and the largest airline introduced by the Azerbaijan government. Azal Airlines has been the flag carrier of Azerbaijan for many years and has paved the way for international flight passage. The headquarters lies in Baku, and all the flight operations are carried out from Heydar Aliyev International Airport. The airline provides international flights to different continents around the world, including Asia, the CIS, and Europe. With its 35 latest generation fleet, Azal Airlines aims to provide luxury and comfort in one go.

Flyadeal
Flyadeal is Saudi Arabia’s low-fare airline dedicated to providing affordable travel options while maintaining quality and convenience. Since its first flight on September 23, 2017, Flyadeal has served over twelve million passengers. Operating as a sister company of Saudi Airlines, Flyadeal is based in Jeddah and caters to a wide range of domestic and regional routes.

Why Bookme?
We are Pakistan's no.1 E-ticketing platform. We let you pre-book the best deals on your tickets for Movies, Bus Travel, Flights, Train Journeys, and Events. You no longer have to stand in lines and can purchase your tickets from the comfort of your phone using a variety of digital payment methods. Get your ticket confirmations instantly via SMS and Email.

Why Bookme?
We are Pakistan's no.1 E-ticketing platform. We let you pre-book the best deals on your tickets for Movies, Bus Travel, Flights, Train Journeys, and Events. You no longer have to stand in lines and can purchase your tickets from the comfort of your phone using a variety of digital payment methods. Get your ticket confirmations instantly via SMS and Email.

Why Bookme?
We are Pakistan's no.1 E-ticketing platform. We let you pre-book the best deals on your tickets for Movies, Bus Travel, Flights, Train Journeys, and Events. You no longer have to stand in lines and can purchase your tickets from the comfort of your phone using a variety of digital payment methods. Get your ticket confirmations instantly via SMS and Email.

Why Bookme?
We are Pakistan's no.1 E-ticketing platform. We let you pre-book the best deals on your tickets for Movies, Bus Travel, Flights, Train Journeys, and Events. You no longer have to stand in lines and can purchase your tickets from the comfort of your phone using a variety of digital payment methods. Get your ticket confirmations instantly via SMS and Email.

Why Bookme?
We are Pakistan's no.1 E-ticketing platform. We let you pre-book the best deals on your tickets for Movies, Bus Travel, Flights, Train Journeys, and Events. You no longer have to stand in lines and can purchase your tickets from the comfort of your phone using a variety of digital payment methods. Get your ticket confirmations instantly via SMS and Email.

Why Bookme?
We are Pakistan's no.1 E-ticketing platform. We let you pre-book the best deals on your tickets for Movies, Bus Travel, Flights, Train Journeys, and Events. You no longer have to stand in lines and can purchase your tickets from the comfort of your phone using a variety of digital payment methods. Get your ticket confirmations instantly via SMS and Email.
